</li><li><p>No certain information has been revealed until now about Santa Claus. It is just broadly known that Santa Claus who is making his tour around the world with his sledge and reindeers (including Rudolph) will put in gifts in the socks hung by chimney by the kind children.</p>
</li><li><p>As it can be conjectured by a document found somewhere in Germany which looked like a Dairy of Santa Claus, it seems like even Santa Claus does not know when and why he started to giving our presents to children.</p>

</li><li><p>Following is a page from his dairy about the dream.</p>

</li><li><p>Year XXXX / Date unknown</p>
</li><li><p>I had the same dream again today. Like always, it was #b6th of December#k and it looked like somewhere in Turkey. I was hunting in the sky with my flying horse. I hunted with my friends and I think they are some kinds of GOD. I felt as if they are my subordinates because they kept calling me <strong>Odin</strong> and me being a GOD leading them.</p>
</li><li><p>Tired from hunting for a long time, we decided to take a rest on the roof of a house. It was weird to see that there were #bboots#k hung by the chimney which were coming out from the roof tops. More surprisingly, there were full of Carrot, Grass and sugar inside the boots as if they knew that we will be taking a rest there. We really appreciated their kind effort and spirit so we have filled the boots with candies and gifts and left for the hunting again.</p>
</li><li><p>One strange thing is that my followers call me Odin but when I go across the lands and reach Germany, they call me <strong>Saint Nicolas</strong>. In Netherlands, they also call me <strong>SinterKlass</strong>. It's funny that all of these names sound like my original name, Santa Claus.</p>
</li><li><p>BTW, my dream always ends with Director of Sales, Johnson appearing and...(Ellipsis)</p>

</li>        </ul>

Most of his face is covered with his beard that it is only his eyes we can actually see. However, since he is always smiling, it is only Mrs. Claus who has clearly seen the eyes of Santa Claus.</p>

</li><li><p>During off-Christmas season, Santa Claus usually writes back the letters from children all over the world and also takes a good care of reindeers as well as the sledge.</p>

And then he arranges the stocks from last year and pays the present company.</p>
</li><li><p>In fact, this off Christmas season is even busier than Christmas season as preparation is getting harder and harder every year he gets old. Santa Claus is always smiling and happy to eyes of Children as he is bringing dreams and hopes to the world but according to Mrs. Claus, there certainly is suffering and loneliness that Santa Claus should endure. Whenever he is feeling blue, he wouldn't tell his wife but <strong>he would go to a big tree in Happy Ville</strong> and take a rest for few hours.</p>
</li><li><p>Recently, more and more children are not starting to believe in Santa Claus anymore and lesser and lesser letter are addressed to Santa Claus every year from Maple World. Mrs. Claus says that this is making him lose his motivation. However, if many Maplers believe in Santa Clause and have confidence that he is coming to town, Santa Claus will find his will again and bring a Happy Christmas in Maple World.</p>
</li>        </ul>

</li><li><p><strong>Encyclopedia Volume 6</strong></p>
</li><li><p><strong>Appendix : Santa Claus town in Finland</strong></p>
</li><li><p>According to Maple Herald, Santa Claus lives in a town called Rovaniemi in Finland. In here, Santa Claus prepares for the next Christmas and maintains the sledge as well as takes care of reindeers too.</p>
</li><li><p>Santa Claus and a lot of people who are helping Santa Claus live in this town. As it gets close to Christmas, millions of letters start to arrive to Santa Claus from all over the world and he writes back every single letters back.</p>
</li><li><p>If there are children who want anything from Santa Claus can always write to him to the address below and Santa Claus will write the children back wherever the letter is from.</p>
</li><li><p>So, if there are a Maplers out there wishing something from Santa Claus, we recommend you to write a letter to the following address.</p>

<p><strong>Santa Claus' Main Post Office, 96930 Napapiiri, Finland</strong></p>
</li>        </ul>
      </td>
    </tr>
  </table>
</div>  </div>
